\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01110}01110\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{def\ }mcc\_safe(y\_true,\ y\_pred):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01111}01111\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ conf\_matrix\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceconfusion__matrix}{confusion\_matrix}}(y\_true,\ y\_pred)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01112}01112\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ true\_pos\ =\ conf\_matrix[1,\ 1]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01113}01113\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ false\_pos\ =\ conf\_matrix[1,\ 0]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01114}01114\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ false\_neg\ =\ conf\_matrix[0,\ 1]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01115}01115\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n\_points\ =\ len(y\_true)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01116}01116\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ pos\_rate\ =\ (true\_pos\ +\ false\_neg)\ /\ n\_points}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01117}01117\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ activity\ =\ (true\_pos\ +\ false\_pos)\ /\ n\_points}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01118}01118\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ mcc\_numerator\ =\ true\_pos\ /\ n\_points\ -\/\ pos\_rate\ *\ activity}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01119}01119\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ mcc\_denominator\ =\ activity\ *\ pos\_rate\ *\ (1\ -\/\ activity)\ *\ (1\ -\/\ pos\_rate)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01120}01120\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ mcc\_numerator\ /\ np.sqrt(mcc\_denominator)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01121}01121\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01122}01122\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{def\ }random\_ys(n\_points):\ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ binary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01123}01123\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\_true\ =\ rng.random\_sample(n\_points)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01125}01125\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\_true\ =\ x\_true\ >\ 0.5}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__classification_8py_source_l01126}01126\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\_pred\ =\ x\_pred\ >\ 0.5}
